[5113] [26.03.2021 05:48:10 UTC-05:00] Indr

I encourage everyone to think twice before trying to find solutions. The puzzle is badly designed. There are serious flaws and this comes from someone who has worked with _hush hush_ data all his life. 

Just two examples.  I have  found many more. 

1. When OP_data (part of the puzzle) was added in TX for the 'causality' brain wallet, it was done on the compressed side - 1Jqq37KkZEt4F3Dt6qXdtyiMEFBBdawbkJ – The puzzle makers did not even check to see that the uncompressed address was already created in 2013. I guess they found out after the puzzle was made public [this alone adds unplanned and unnecessary confusion and for me it shows bad design]

2.  You can read all the public OP_data directly on the blockchain instead of going through whatever phase and whatever ciphers [this was also unplanned] How? Just use a blockchain parser and search for 47534d472e (ASCI for their website). Sample at:   blockchain [dot] info/block/000000000000000000078fbc77e0c5e2b10ade8880a265c140e6e36d29b2da29?format=hex ] --- this is only for a single block but of course it's all there...

This can only prove that they realized this puzzle cannot be solved without them frequently interfering in the solving process. My sincere advice to them: please, do not provide any more clues to these poor people.  These clues [which are different puzzles altogether!] cannot help unexperienced solvers with their thinking process. And the users who think they have understood the hints just because they got onto the next phase they will be in for quite a surprise.

I wanted to say nothing, but I can see so many are messaging me [please don’t] and struggling and it’s all because of a bad design not because the puzzle is hard - in popular layman terms. I was here to send a professional warning to all those spending too much time on this – it's a nice try but it was not built well and you will waste more time than you think because the construct is flawed. 

Just ask yourself: what if there were no clues at all? None. Just the puzzle. For how long people would still be stuck? Years perhaps. Why? Because you NEED clues and that is bad design.  

Do something better with your time. Have fun, read and work hard. Be kind to others, it will pay off. 

As for this puzzle, even if you get to a so called final stage trust me, you will hit the biggest wall of all and you will be quite disappointed.
